### 1.3 CÃ¡c khÃ¡i niá»‡m cÆ¡ báº£n (Glossary)

#### **PCTL (Percentile)**
```
Äá»‹nh nghÄ©a: Vá»‹ trÃ­ cá»§a giÃ¡ trá»‹ hiá»‡n táº¡i trong phÃ¢n phá»‘i lá»‹ch sá»­

CÃ¡ch Ä‘á»c:
â”œâ”€ PCTL = 50: BÃ¬nh thÆ°á»ng (median)
â”œâ”€ PCTL = 80+: Cao báº¥t thÆ°á»ng (top 20%)
â””â”€ PCTL = 20-: Tháº¥p báº¥t thÆ°á»ng (bottom 20%)

LÆ°u Ã½:
- "highIsBad" metrics (CPI, Tight_idx): PCTL cao = Xáº¤U
- "highIsGood" metrics (GDP, Growth): PCTL cao = Tá»T

VÃ­ dá»¥:
CPI PCTL = 85 â†’ Láº¡m phÃ¡t trong top 15% cao nháº¥t lá»‹ch sá»­ â†’ ğŸ”´ Rá»¦I RO
GDP PCTL = 85 â†’ GDP trong top 15% máº¡nh nháº¥t lá»‹ch sá»­ â†’ ğŸŸ¢ Tá»T
```

#### **A. CPI YoY (Consumer Price Index - Year over Year)**

**Äá»‹nh nghÄ©a:**
```
CPI YoY = (CPI thÃ¡ng nÃ y - CPI cÃ¹ng ká»³ nÄƒm ngoÃ¡i) / CPI nÄƒm ngoÃ¡i Ã— 100%

VÃ­ dá»¥:

```

**CÃ¡ch Ä‘á»c:**

```
â”œâ”€ CPI 4-6%: Ãp lá»±c tÄƒng (cáº§n theo dÃµi)
```

### 3.4 Giáº£i thÃ­ch tá»«ng chá»‰ sá»‘

#### **A. Tight_idx (Chá»‰ sá»‘ tháº¯t cháº·t) - QUAN TRá»ŒNG NHáº¤T**

**CÃ´ng thá»©c:**
```
Real Rate Gap = Real Rate - EMA(Real Rate, 12 thÃ¡ng)
Î” Interbank = Interbank[t] - Interbank[t-1]

Tight_idx = Z-score(Real Rate Gap) + 0.5 Ã— Z-score(Î” Interbank)
```

**CÃ¡ch Ä‘á»c:**
```
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¬â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
â”‚ Tight_idx  â”‚ Ã nghÄ©a                              â”‚
```

#### **B. Policy Gap (Taylor Rule Gap)**

**CÃ´ng thá»©c Taylor Rule:**
```
i* = r* + Ï€ + Ï†_Ï€ Ã— (Ï€ - Ï€*) + Ï†_y Ã— GDP_gap

Default parameters:
- r* = 1.0% (neutral real rate)
- Ï€* = 4.0% (inflation target)
- Ï†_Ï€ = 0.5 (inflation response)
- Ï†_y = 0.5 (output gap response)

Policy Gap = i_policy_actual - i*
```

**VÃ­ dá»¥ tÃ­nh toÃ¡n:**
```
Giáº£ sá»­:
- Ï€ (CPI) = 3.8%
- GDP gap = +0.5%
- r* = 1.0%
- Ï€* = 4.0%

â†’ i* = 1.0 + 3.8 + 0.5Ã—(3.8-4.0) + 0.5Ã—0.5
     = 1.0 + 3.8 - 0.1 + 0.25
     = 4.95%

Náº¿u i_policy_actual = 4.5%:
â†’ Policy Gap = 4.5 - 4.95 = -0.45% (ná»›i hÆ¡n "há»£p lÃ½")
```

**Diá»…n giáº£i:**

#### **D. Grow_idx (Growth Index - Z-score)**

**CÃ´ng thá»©c:**
```
Grow_idx = Z-score(GDP_gap, lookback=40 quÃ½)

Z-score = (GDP_gap - mean(GDP_gap, 40)) / stdev(GDP_gap, 40)

Vá»›i robust z-score (winsorized):
- Clip outliers trÆ°á»›c
- TÃ­nh mean/std trÃªn clipped data
```

**CÃ¡ch Ä‘á»c:**
```
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”¬â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
â”‚ Grow_idx   â”‚ Ã nghÄ©a (standardized)                â”‚

â”‚ > 2.0      â”‚ ğŸ”µ Trong top 2.5% máº¡nh nháº¥t           â”‚
```

### 4.8 Decision Matrix


### 5.6 Quality Score - Äo cháº¥t lÆ°á»£ng dá»¯ liá»‡u

**CÃ´ng thá»©c:**
```
Step 1: TÃ­nh robust z-score cho má»—i tenor
z_2y = robust_z(VN02Y, 120 days)
z_5y = robust_z(VN05Y, 120 days)
z_10y = robust_z(VN10Y, 120 days)

Step 2: TÃ­nh dispersion (Ä‘á»™ phÃ¢n tÃ¡n)
mean_z = (z_2y + z_5y + z_10y) / 3
variance_z = [(z_2y - mean_z)Â² + (z_5y - mean_z)Â² + (z_10y - mean_z)Â²] / 6
distortion = sqrt(variance_z)

Step 3: Quality score
distortion_clamped = min(1.2, max(0, distortion))
quality = 100 - (distortion_clamped / 1.2) Ã— 100

Step 4: Label
HIGHQ: quality >= 75%
MEDQ: quality >= 50%
LOWQ: quality < 50%
```

### 5.7 Stress Index - Äo cÄƒng tháº³ng thá»‹ trÆ°á»ng

**CÃ´ng thá»©c:**
```
Step 1: Stress components
level_pct = percentrank(Level, 120 days)

slope_risk = if Slope <= 0:
                100%  // Inverted = max stress
             else:
                100 - percentrank(Slope, 120 days)

Step 2: Raw stress
Stress_raw = (level_pct + slope_risk) / 2

Step 3: Adjusted stress
Stress_adj = Stress_raw Ã— (Quality / 100)
```

### 5.8 YC Research vs VNINDEX - Lead/Lag Analysis

**Má»¥c tiÃªu:** Kiá»ƒm tra xem YC Stress cÃ³ dá»± bÃ¡o Ä‘Æ°á»£c VNINDEX khÃ´ng?

**Methodology:**
```
Step 1: TÃ­nh VNINDEX log return
vnx_ret = log(VNINDEX[t] / VNINDEX[t-1])

Step 2: Winsorize return (clip outliers)
mean_ret = sma(vnx_ret, 120)
std_ret = stdev(vnx_ret, 120)
vnx_ret_clipped = clip(vnx_ret, mean - 3*std, mean + 3*std)

Step 3: TÃ­nh correlation vá»›i 3 lags
Lag1 (1 day): corr(Stress_adj[t], vnx_ret_clipped[t+1])
Lag5 (1 week): corr(Stress_adj[t], vnx_ret_clipped[t+5])
Lag20 (1 month): corr(Stress_adj[t], vnx_ret_clipped[t+20])

Step 4: Select BestLag
BestLag = lag vá»›i |correlation| cao nháº¥t

Step 5: TÃ­nh Beta (OLS)
Beta = cov(Stress, Return) / var(Stress)
RÂ² = correlationÂ²

Step 6: Lag Stability
Track BestLag trong 60 ngÃ y gáº§n nháº¥t
Stability = % thá»i gian BestLag khÃ´ng Ä‘á»•i
```

**Diá»…n giáº£i káº¿t quáº£:**
```
â”Œâ”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”
```

### 6.3 Risk Score Calculation - CÃ´ng thá»©c 3 Layers

#### **Layer 1: Funding Pressure (Ãp lá»±c thanh khoáº£n)**

**Components:**
```
1. Stress High (Tight_idx trigger):
   - Dynamic: z(Tight_idx) > 1.0
   - Percentile: Tight_idx > p85
   - Static: Tight_idx > 1.5
   â†’ Score: +w_stress (default 2.5)

2. DXY Stress:
   - DXY > threshold (default 105)
   â†’ Score: +w_dxy (default 1.0)

Layer1_Score = Stress_score + DXY_score
Max Layer1 = 2.5 + 1.0 = 3.5
```

**Ã nghÄ©a:**
```
Layer 1 lÃ  "red alert" layer - CÄƒn báº£n nháº¥t
- Náº¿u thanh khoáº£n cÄƒng â†’ Táº¥t cáº£ asset classes bá»‹ áº£nh hÆ°á»Ÿng
- KhÃ´ng thá»ƒ "diversify away" funding stress
- Must reduce risk NGAY náº¿u Layer 1 trigger

Example:
Tight_idx = 2.1 (PCTL 90) â†’ Stress trigger
DXY = 106 â†’ DXY trigger
â†’ Layer1 = 2.5 + 1.0 = 3.5 (MAX)
â†’ Chiáº¿m 3.5/14.5 = 24% risk score
```

---

#### **Layer 2: Cycle Risk (Rá»§i ro chu ká»³)**

**Components:**
```
1. YC Inversion (Curve_inversion):
   - Dynamic: z(Slope) < -1.0
   - Percentile: Slope < p15
   - Static: Slope < 0
   â†’ Score: +w_curve (default 2.0)

2. Growth Low:
   - Dynamic: z(GDP_gap) < -1.0
   - Percentile: GDP_gap < p15
   - Static: GDP_gap < 0
   â†’ Score: +w_growth (default 1.5)

3. Spread Warning (Long-short spread):
   - Dynamic: z(long_short_spread) < -1.0
   - Percentile: spread < p15
   - Static: spread < 0.5%
   â†’ Score: +w_spread (default 1.5)

Layer2_Score = Curve + Growth + Spread
Max Layer2 = 2.0 + 1.5 + 1.5 = 5.0
```

**Ã nghÄ©a:**
```
Layer 2 lÃ  "structural" layer - Chu ká»³ dÃ i háº¡n
- YC inversion: Recession predictor máº¡nh nháº¥t
- Growth low: GDP yáº¿u â†’ Earnings pressure
- Spread háº¹p: Term premium tháº¥p â†’ Complacency

Äáº·c Ä‘iá»ƒm:
- ThÆ°á»ng cÃ³ lead time 6-18 thÃ¡ng
- KhÃ´ng cáº§n action gáº¥p nhÆ° Layer 1
- NhÆ°ng cáº§n chuáº©n bá»‹ dáº§n

Example:
YC inverted: Slope = -0.3% â†’ +2.0
Growth OK: GDP_gap = +0.3% â†’ +0.0
Spread háº¹p: 0.4% â†’ +1.5
â†’ Layer2 = 3.5 / 5.0
```

---

#### **Layer 3: External Factors (Yáº¿u tá»‘ ngoáº¡i vi)**

**Components:**
```
1. International Warning:
   - VN-US spread < threshold
   â†’ Score: +w_intl (default 1.5)

2. Inflation High:
   - CPI > Target + 1%
   â†’ Score: +w_inflation (default 1.5)

3. Drivers High (PPI/FX/Oil):
   - Drivers_idx elevated
   â†’ Score: +w_drv (default 1.0)

4. Credit High (náº¿u báº­t):
   - M2 gap > threshold
   â†’ Score: +w_credit (default 1.0)

5. External Stress:
   - Miscellaneous shocks
   â†’ Score: +1.0

Layer3_Score = Intl + Infl + Drivers + Credit + External
Max Layer3 = 1.5 + 1.5 + 1.0 + 1.0 + 1.0 = 6.0
```

**Ã nghÄ©a:**
```
Layer 3 lÃ  "slow-burn" layer - TÃ­ch lÅ©y dáº§n
- CÃ¡c yáº¿u tá»‘ nÃ y khÃ´ng gÃ¢y crisis ngay
- NhÆ°ng tÃ­ch lÅ©y lÃ¢u ngÃ y â†’ TÄƒng fragility
- Quan trá»ng cho medium-term (3-12 thÃ¡ng)

Example:
Intl OK: VN-US = 2.0% â†’ +0.0
Inflation high: CPI = 4.5% â†’ +1.5
Drivers high: PPI/FX spike â†’ +1.0
Credit OK: M2 gap normal â†’ +0.0
â†’ Layer3 = 2.5 / 6.0
```

---

#### **Total Risk Score**

**CÃ´ng thá»©c:**
```
Total_Score = Layer1 + Layer2 + Layer3
Max_Score = 3.5 + 5.0 + 6.0 = 14.5

Risk_pct = (Total_Score / Max_Score) Ã— 100%

Valuation Adjustment:
IF is_cheap = true (VNINDEX < MA200 Ã— 0.80)
   AND Risk_pct > 60%:
   Risk_pct = Risk_pct Ã— 0.85  // Giáº£m 15%

Final_Risk = Risk_pct after adjustment
```

**Example tÃ­nh toÃ¡n:**
```
Scenario:
Layer1 = 1.5 (only Stress, no DXY)
Layer2 = 3.5 (YC + Spread, no Growth)
Layer3 = 2.5 (Inflation + Drivers)
Total = 7.5

Risk_pct = 7.5 / 14.5 Ã— 100% = 51.7%

Valuation:
VNINDEX = 1,150
MA200 = 1,300
Distance = 1,150/1,300 = 0.885 > 0.80 (not cheap)
â†’ No adjustment

Final Risk = 51.7% â†’ Bucket B2
```

**Stability Score:**
```
Stability = (Sum of diagonal) / (Total transitions)

Example:
Diagonal sum = 65% + 60% + 50% + 55% + 55% = 285%
Total = 193 transitions across all buckets

High stability (>60%):
- Buckets "sticky"
- Ãt thay Ä‘á»•i Ä‘á»™t ngá»™t
- CÃ³ thá»ƒ hold longer

Low stability (<40%):
- Buckets volatile
- Hay chuyá»ƒn
- Rebalance thÆ°á»ng xuyÃªn hÆ¡n
```

**Bucket Duration:**

### **7.2. CÃ´ng Thá»©c TÃ­nh ToÃ¡n**

**CÃ¡ch Äá»c:**

#### **B. M2 Gap (ChÃªnh Lá»‡ch M2)**

**Ã NghÄ©a:**

#### **C. Credit_idx (Chá»‰ Sá»‘ TÃ­n Dá»¥ng)**

### **8.5. LÆ°u Ã Quan Trá»ng: PhÃ¢n Ká»³ Giáº£ (False Divergence)**

**4 ThÃ nh Pháº§n Ãp Lá»±c:**

### **9.2. CÃ´ng Thá»©c TÃ­nh ToÃ¡n**

**Ã NghÄ©a:**

| **B0**     | 0-20%    | ğŸŸ¢ Tech, Small-cap, Growth | ğŸ”´ Utilities, Gold     | Táº¥n cÃ´ng: Growth > Value  |

### **11.2. CÃ´ng Thá»©c TÃ­nh ToÃ¡n**

#### **A. US Level (Má»©c LÃ£i Suáº¥t Trung BÃ¬nh)**
```pine

```

**Ã NghÄ©a:**
- `US_Level > 5%`: ğŸ”´ **Ráº¤T CAO** - Fed tháº¯t cháº·t máº¡nh, dÃ²ng vá»‘n rÃºt khá»i EM
- `US_Level 4-5%`: ğŸŸ¡ **CAO** - Ãp lá»±c vá»«a pháº£i

#### **B. US Slope (Äá»™ Dá»‘c ÄÆ°á»ng Cong)**

#### **TÃ­nh Äiá»ƒm Tá»•ng Há»£p (Scoring System)**

```

   - +2: Ráº¥t tÃ­ch cá»±c (Strong Buy)

```

**VÃ­ Dá»¥ TÃ­nh Äiá»ƒm:**
